To find out how much you have to pay for each pack after the discount, subtract the discount from the original price.\n4. Therefore, the price you have to pay for each pack is 76 - 25.\n5. Performing the subtraction, we get 76 - 25 = 51.\n\nThe answer is 51 dollars."

Therefore, the total number of children on the bus after 82 got on is 28 + 82 = 110 children.\n4. After some children got off, there were 30 children left on the bus.\n5. To find out how many children got off the bus, we subtract the number of children remaining from the total number of children after 82 got on: 110 - 30 = 80 children got off the bus.\n6. "Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Nell originally had 309 baseball cards.\n2. Nell originally had 356 Ace cards.\n3. The total number of cards Nell originally had is 309 + 356 = 665 cards.\n4. After giving some cards to Jeff, Nell has 415 cards left.\n5. To find out how many cards Nell gave to Jeff, we subtract the number of cards she has now from the original total: 665 - 415 = 250 cards.\n6. We need to determine how many more baseball cards than Ace cards Nell has now.\n7. Let \\( x \\) be the number of baseball cards Nell has now, and \\( y \\) be the number of Ace cards she has now.\n8. We know that \\( x + y = 415 \\).\n9. We also know that the difference between the original number of baseball and Ace cards is \\( 309 - 356 = -47 \\).\n10. Since Nell gave away 250 cards, the difference in the number of baseball and Ace cards she has now should be the same as the original difference, which is -47.\n11. Therefore, \\( x - y = -47 \\).\n12. We have two equations:\n    - \\( x + y = 415 \\)\n    - \\( x - y = -47 \\)\n13. Solving these equations simultaneously:\n    - Add the two equations: \\( (x + y) + (x - y) = 415 - 47 \\)\n    - This simplifies to \\( 2x = 368 \\)\n    - Solving for \\( x \\), we get \\( x = 184 \\).\n14. Substitute \\( x = 184 \\) back into the equation \\( x + y = 415 \\):\n    - \\( 184 + y = 415 \\)\n    - Solving for \\( y \\), we get \\( y = 231 \\).\n15. Therefore, Nell has 184 baseball cards and 231 Ace cards.\n16. The difference in the number of baseball cards and Ace cards is \\( 184 - 231 = -47 \\).\n\nThe answer is that Nell has 47 more Ace cards than baseball cards."

Therefore, the total number of green and yellow peaches is 14 + 6.\n5. Performing the addition, we get 14 + 6 = 20.\n\nThe answer is 20."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Total bird families living near the mountain: 89\n2. Bird families that flew away for winter: 60\n3. To find the number of bird families that stayed behind, we subtract the number of families that flew away from the total number of families.\n   - Bird families that stayed behind: 89 - 60 = 29\n4. To find how many more bird families flew away than those that stayed, we subtract the number of families that stayed from the number of families that flew away.\n   - Difference between bird families that flew away and those that stayed: 60 - 29 = 31\n\nThe answer is 31."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. There are now 13 orchids in the vase.\n2. There are now 3 roses in the vase.\n3. To find out how many more orchids than roses are in the vase, we subtract the number of roses from the number of orchids.\n4. Therefore, the number of more orchids than roses is 13 - 3.\n5. Performing the subtraction, we get 13 - 3 = 10.\n\nThe answer is 10. There are 10 more orchids than roses in the vase now."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. The number of visitors on the day Rachel visited the Buckingham Palace was 661.\n2. The number of visitors on the previous day was 600.\n3. To find out how many more visitors visited on the day Rachel visited compared to the previous day, we need to subtract the number of visitors on the previous day from the number of visitors on the day Rachel visited.\n4. Therefore, the number of more visitors on the day Rachel visited is 661 - 600.\n5. Performing the subtraction, we get 661 - 600 = 61.\n\nThe answer is 61."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Initially, the waiter had 12 customers.\n2. 15 customers left.\n3. To find out how many customers remained after some left, we subtract the number of customers who left from the initial number of customers.\n4. Therefore, the number of customers remaining after some left is 12 - 15.\n5. Performing the subtraction, we get 12 - 15 = -3. This indicates that the number of customers who left exceeded the initial number of customers, resulting in a negative count, which is not possible in this context.\n6. However, since 14 new customers arrived, we add these new customers to the remaining count.\n7. Therefore, the number of customers the waiter currently has is -3 + 14.\n8. Performing the addition, we get -3 + 14 = 11.\n\nThe answer is 11."

Therefore, the number of necklaces Emily can make is 6 divided by 3.\n5. Performing the division, we get 6 / 3 = 2.\n\nThe answer is that Emily can make 2 necklaces."

Therefore, she has already put in 11 - 9 = 2 cups of flour.\n\nThe answer is 2 cups of flour."

Lewis works for 73 harvest seasons.\n5. To find out how much he earns in total for 73 seasons, we multiply his earnings per season by the number of seasons.\n   - Total earnings = $302,611 * 73\n   - Performing the multiplication, we get $302,611 * 73 = $22,086,603.\n\nThe answer is $22,086,603."

"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Initially, there were 36 children on the bus.\n2. 68 children got off the bus.\n3. After some children got on the bus, there were 12 children altogether on the bus.\n\nTo find out how many children got on the bus, we can set up the equation:\n\n- Initial number of children on the bus: 36\n- Number of children who got off the bus: 68\n- Number of children who got on the bus: \\( x \\)\n- Final number of children on the bus: 12\n\nThe equation is:\n\\[ 36 - 68 + x = 12 \\]\n\nSolving for \\( x \\):\n\\[ 36 - 68 + x = 12 \\]\n\\[ -32 + x = 12 \\]\n\\[ x = 12 + 32 \\]\n\\[ x = 44 \\]\n\nSo, 44 children got on the bus.\n\nNow, to find out how many more children got off the bus than those that got on:\n- Number of children who got off: 68\n- Number of children who got on: 44\n\nThe difference is:\n\\[ 68 - 44 = 24 \\]\n\nTherefore, 24 more children got off the bus than those that got on. The answer is 24."

Performing the subtraction, we get $16 - $8 = $8.\n\nThe answer is that Edward spent $8 more on books than on pens."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Each necklace requires 8 beads.\n2. Emily has a total of 16 beads.\n3. To find out how many necklaces Emily can make, we need to divide the total number of beads by the number of beads required for each necklace.\n4. Therefore, the number of necklaces Emily can make is 16 divided by 8.\n5. Performing the division, we get 16 / 8 = 2.\n\nThe answer is 2. Emily can make 2 necklaces."

To find out how much the candy bar cost, we need to subtract the amount of money Dan had left from the amount he initially had.\n4. Therefore, the cost of the candy bar is $4 - $3.\n5. Performing the subtraction, we get $4 - $3 = $1.\n\nThe answer is $1."

Performing the subtraction, we get 253 - 70 = 183.\n\nThe answer is 183. Paul had 183 crayons left by the end of the school year."

"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Jesse's room requires a carpet of 10 square feet to cover it.\n2. The room is 2 feet wide.\n3. The area of a rectangle (which is the shape of the room) is calculated by multiplying its width by its length.\n4. We know the area of the room is 10 square feet and the width is 2 feet.\n5. To find the length of the room, we use the formula for the area of a rectangle: Area = Width  Length.\n6. Plugging in the known values, we have 10 = 2  Length.\n7. To solve for the length, divide both sides of the equation by 2: Length = 10 / 2.\n8. Performing the division, we get Length = 5.\n\nThe answer is that the length of Jesse's room is 5 feet."

After some children got on the bus, there were 12 children altogether on the bus.\n\nTo find out how many children got on the bus, we can set up the equation:\n\n- Initial number of children on the bus: 36\n- Number of children who got off the bus: 68\n- Number of children who got on the bus: \\( x \\)\n- Final number of children on the bus: 12\n\nThe equation is:\n\\[ 36 - 68 + x = 12 \\]\n\nSolving for \\( x \\):\n\\[ 36 - 68 + x = 12 \\]\n\\[ -32 + x = 12 \\]\n\\[ x = 12 + 32 \\]\n\\[ x = 44 \\]\n\nSo, 44 children got on the bus.\n\nNow, to find out how many more children got off the bus than those that got on:\n- Number of children who got off: 68\n- Number of children who got on: 44\n\nThe difference is:\n\\[ 68 - 44 = 24 \\]\n\nTherefore, 24 more children got off the bus than those that got on. Let \\( x \\) be the number of bottle caps Danny had initially.\n6. After finding and discarding bottle caps, the equation for his current collection is:\n   \\[\n   x + 63 - 51 = 33\n   \\]\n7. "Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Jesse's room requires a carpet of 10 square feet to cover it.\n2. The room is 2 feet wide.\n3. The area of a rectangle (which is the shape of the room) is calculated by multiplying its width by its length.\n4. We know the area of the room is 10 square feet and the width is 2 feet.\n5. To find the length of the room, we use the formula for the area of a rectangle: Area = Width  Length.\n6. Plugging in the known values, we have 10 = 2  Length.\n7. To solve for the length, divide both sides of the equation by 2: Length = 10 / 2.\n8. Performing the division, we get Length = 5.\n\nThe answer is that the length of Jesse's room is 5 feet."

To find out how much Jessie weighed before she started jogging, we need to add the total weight loss to her current weight.\n6. Therefore, Jessie's weight before she started jogging was 9 + 202 = 211 kilograms.\n\nThe answer is 211 kilograms."

She needs to add 9 cups of flour and 6 cups of sugar.\n8. Therefore, she needs to add 9 - 6 = 3 more cups of flour than sugar.\n\nThe answer is 3 more cups of flour than cups of sugar."

Then, Jerry removed 7 action figures, so the number becomes \\( x + 2 - 7 \\).\n7. To find out how many more books he sold than he bought, we subtract the number of books he bought from the number of books he sold.\n9. Therefore, the number of more books he sold than he bought is 48 - 42 = 6.\n\nThe answer is 6."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Allan and Jake together brought a total of 3 balloons to the park.\n2. Allan brought 2 balloons.\n3. To find out how many balloons Jake brought, we subtract the number of balloons Allan brought from the total number of balloons.\n4. Therefore, the number of balloons Jake brought is 3 - 2.\n5. Performing the subtraction, we get 3 - 2 = 1.\n\nThe answer is 1. Jake brought 1 balloon to the park."

"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. They harvest 66 sacks of oranges per day.\n2. Each sack contains 25 oranges.\n3. To find out how many oranges are harvested per day, we multiply the number of sacks by the number of oranges per sack.\n   - Oranges per day = 66 sacks/day * 25 oranges/sack = 1,650 oranges/day.\n4. The harvest period is 87 days.\n5. To find the total number of oranges harvested over 87 days, we multiply the number of oranges harvested per day by the number of days.\n   - Total oranges = 1,650 oranges/day * 87 days = 143,550 oranges.\n\nThe answer is 143,550 oranges."

"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Initially, there were 13 roses in the vase.\n2. Jessica's flower garden originally had a total of 12 roses.\n3. After Jessica added some roses to the vase, there are now 21 roses in the vase.\n4. To find out how many roses Jessica cut from her garden, we subtract the initial number of roses in the vase from the current number of roses in the vase.\n5. Therefore, the number of roses Jessica cut from her garden is 21 - 13.\n6. Performing the subtraction, we get 21 - 13 = 8.\n7. Jessica cut 8 roses from her garden.\n8. To find out how many roses are left in the garden, we subtract the number of roses Jessica cut from the total number of roses originally in the garden.\n9. Therefore, the number of roses left in the garden is 12 - 8.\n10. Performing the subtraction, we get 12 - 8 = 4.\n\nThe answer is that Jessica cut 8 roses from her garden, and there are 4 roses left in the garden."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Jerry added 2 more action figures to the shelf.\n2. Jerry removed 7 of the old action figures from the shelf.\n3. There are currently 10 action figures on the shelf.\n\nTo find out how many action figures Jerry initially had, we need to consider the changes made to the initial number:\n\n4. Let \\( x \\) be the initial number of action figures on the shelf.\n5. After adding 2 action figures, the number becomes \\( x + 2 \\).\n6. Then, Jerry removed 7 action figures, so the number becomes \\( x + 2 - 7 \\).\n7. We know that after these changes, there are 10 action figures on the shelf.\n\nTherefore, we can set up the equation:\n\n\\[ x + 2 - 7 = 10 \\]\n\n8. Simplify the equation:\n\n\\[ x - 5 = 10 \\]\n\n9. Solve for \\( x \\) by adding 5 to both sides:\n\n\\[ x = 10 + 5 \\]\n\n10. Therefore, \\( x = 15 \\).\n\nThe answer is that Jerry initially had 15 action figures on the shelf."

Therefore, the number of cards Nell has left is 242 - 136.\n5. Performing the subtraction, we get 242 - 136 = 106.\n\nThe answer is 106. Nell has 106 cards left."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Helen baked 90 chocolate chip cookies yesterday.\n2. Helen baked 484 chocolate chip cookies this morning.\n3. To find the total number of chocolate chip cookies Helen baked, we need to add the number of cookies she baked yesterday to the number she baked this morning.\n4. Therefore, the total number of chocolate chip cookies is 90 + 484.\n5. Performing the addition, we get 90 + 484 = 574.\n\nThe answer is 574."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Initially, there were 13 roses in the vase.\n2. Jessica's flower garden originally had a total of 12 roses.\n3. After Jessica added some roses to the vase, there are now 21 roses in the vase.\n4. To find out how many roses Jessica cut from her garden, we subtract the initial number of roses in the vase from the current number of roses in the vase.\n5. Therefore, the number of roses Jessica cut from her garden is 21 - 13.\n6. Performing the subtraction, we get 21 - 13 = 8.\n7. Jessica cut 8 roses from her garden.\n8. To find out how many roses are left in the garden, we subtract the number of roses Jessica cut from the total number of roses originally in the garden.\n9. Therefore, the number of roses left in the garden is 12 - 8.\n10. Performing the subtraction, we get 12 - 8 = 4.\n\nThe answer is that Jessica cut 8 roses from her garden, and there are 4 roses left in the garden."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Jerry added 2 more action figures to the shelf.\n2. Jerry removed 7 of the old action figures from the shelf.\n3. There are currently 10 action figures on the shelf.\n\nTo find out how many action figures Jerry initially had, we need to consider the changes made to the initial number:\n\n4. Let \\( x \\) be the initial number of action figures on the shelf.\n5. After adding 2 action figures, the number becomes \\( x + 2 \\).\n6. Then, Jerry removed 7 action figures, so the number becomes \\( x + 2 - 7 \\).\n7. We know that after these changes, there are 10 action figures on the shelf.\n\nTherefore, we can set up the equation:\n\n\\[ x + 2 - 7 = 10 \\]\n\n8. Simplify the equation:\n\n\\[ x - 5 = 10 \\]\n\n9. Solve for \\( x \\) by adding 5 to both sides:\n\n\\[ x = 10 + 5 \\]\n\n10. Therefore, \\( x = 15 \\).\n\nThe answer is that Jerry initially had 15 action figures on the shelf."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. The book has a total of 23 pages.\n2. The first chapter is 10 pages long.\n\nGiven this information, we can directly determine the number of pages in the first chapter:\n\n3. The first chapter has 10 pages.\n\nThe answer is 10."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Paul initially had 21 books.\n2. He bought 42 new books.\n3. After buying, the total number of books he should have is 21 + 42 = 63 books.\n4. He has 15 books now.\n5. To find out how many books he sold, we subtract the number of books he currently has from the total number of books he should have had.\n6. Therefore, the number of books he sold is 63 - 15 = 48 books.\n7. He bought 42 new books.\n8. To find out how many more books he sold than he bought, we subtract the number of books he bought from the number of books he sold.\n9. Therefore, the number of more books he sold than he bought is 48 - 42 = 6.\n\nThe answer is 6."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Allan and Jake together brought a total of 3 balloons to the park.\n2. Allan brought 2 balloons.\n3. To find out how many balloons Jake brought, we subtract the number of balloons Allan brought from the total number of balloons.\n4. Therefore, the number of balloons Jake brought is 3 - 2.\n5. Performing the subtraction, we get 3 - 2 = 1.\n\nThe answer is 1. Jake brought 1 balloon to the park."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. The total number of students in the school is 270.\n2. Each grade has 5 students.\n3. To find the total number of grades, we need to divide the total number of students by the number of students in each grade.\n4. Therefore, the number of grades is 270 divided by 5.\n5. Performing the division, we get 270 / 5 = 54.\n\nThe answer is 54 grades."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. The total number of kids in Lawrence County is 898,051.\n2. The number of kids who go to camp is 629,424.\n3. To find out how many kids stay home, we need to subtract the number of kids who go to camp from the total number of kids.\n4. Therefore, the number of kids who stay home is 898,051 - 629,424.\n5. Performing the subtraction, we get 898,051 - 629,424 = 268,627.\n\nThe answer is 268,627 kids stay home."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Dave initially had 21 files on his phone.\n2. After deleting some files, he had 7 files left.\n3. To find out how many files Dave deleted, we need to subtract the number of files he has left from the initial number of files.\n4. Therefore, the number of files Dave deleted is 21 - 7.\n5. Performing the subtraction, we get 21 - 7 = 14.\n\nThe answer is 14."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. The total number of cookies is 33.\n2. Each bag contains 11 cookies.\n3. To find the number of bags, we need to divide the total number of cookies by the number of cookies per bag.\n4. Therefore, the number of bags is 33 divided by 11.\n5. Performing the division, we get 33 / 11 = 3.\n\nThe answer is 3 bags."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. They harvest 66 sacks of oranges per day.\n2. Each sack contains 25 oranges.\n3. To find out how many oranges are harvested per day, we multiply the number of sacks by the number of oranges per sack.\n   - Oranges per day = 66 sacks/day * 25 oranges/sack = 1,650 oranges/day.\n4. The harvest period is 87 days.\n5. To find the total number of oranges harvested over 87 days, we multiply the number of oranges harvested per day by the number of days.\n   - Total oranges = 1,650 oranges/day * 87 days = 143,550 oranges.\n\nThe answer is 143,550 oranges."

Let \\( x \\) be the initial number of action figures on the shelf.\n5. After adding 2 action figures, the number becomes \\( x + 2 \\).\n6. Then, Jerry removed 7 action figures, so the number becomes \\( x + 2 - 7 \\).\n7. "Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Fred earned money by delivering newspapers.\n   - He earned 16 dollars from delivering newspapers.\n\n2. Fred also earned money by washing cars.\n   - He earned 74 dollars from washing cars.\n\n3. To find out how much money Fred earned over the weekend, we need to add the amounts he earned from both activities.\n\n4. Therefore, the total amount Fred earned over the weekend is 16 + 74.\n\n5. Performing the addition, we get 16 + 74 = 90.\n\nThe answer is 90 dollars."

Performing the division, we get 14 / 7 = 2.\n\nThe answer is that each bag has 2 cookies."

After Jessica added some roses to the vase, there are now 21 roses in the vase.\n4. To find out how many roses Jessica cut from her garden, we subtract the initial number of roses in the vase from the current number of roses in the vase.\n5. "Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Jerry added 2 more action figures to the shelf.\n2. Jerry removed 7 of the old action figures from the shelf.\n3. There are currently 10 action figures on the shelf.\n\nTo find out how many action figures Jerry initially had, we need to consider the changes made to the initial number:\n\n4. Let \\( x \\) be the initial number of action figures on the shelf.\n5. After adding 2 action figures, the number becomes \\( x + 2 \\).\n6. Then, Jerry removed 7 action figures, so the number becomes \\( x + 2 - 7 \\).\n7. We know that after these changes, there are 10 action figures on the shelf.\n\nTherefore, we can set up the equation:\n\n\\[ x + 2 - 7 = 10 \\]\n\n8. Simplify the equation:\n\n\\[ x - 5 = 10 \\]\n\n9. Solve for \\( x \\) by adding 5 to both sides:\n\n\\[ x = 10 + 5 \\]\n\n10. Therefore, \\( x = 15 \\).\n\nThe answer is that Jerry initially had 15 action figures on the shelf."

"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Allan and Jake together brought a total of 3 balloons to the park.\n2. Allan brought 2 balloons.\n3. To find out how many balloons Jake brought, we subtract the number of balloons Allan brought from the total number of balloons.\n4. Therefore, the number of balloons Jake brought is 3 - 2.\n5. Performing the subtraction, we get 3 - 2 = 1.\n\nThe answer is 1. Jake brought 1 balloon to the park."

To find how many more trees survived than those that died, we subtract the number of trees that died from the number of trees that survived.\n   - Difference = 9 - 2 = 7.\n\nThe answer is 7."

"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Initially, there were 13 roses in the vase.\n2. Jessica's flower garden originally had a total of 12 roses.\n3. After Jessica added some roses to the vase, there are now 21 roses in the vase.\n4. To find out how many roses Jessica cut from her garden, we subtract the initial number of roses in the vase from the current number of roses in the vase.\n5. Therefore, the number of roses Jessica cut from her garden is 21 - 13.\n6. Performing the subtraction, we get 21 - 13 = 8.\n7. Jessica cut 8 roses from her garden.\n8. To find out how many roses are left in the garden, we subtract the number of roses Jessica cut from the total number of roses originally in the garden.\n9. Therefore, the number of roses left in the garden is 12 - 8.\n10. Performing the subtraction, we get 12 - 8 = 4.\n\nThe answer is that Jessica cut 8 roses from her garden, and there are 4 roses left in the garden."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Jerry added 2 more action figures to the shelf.\n2. Jerry removed 7 of the old action figures from the shelf.\n3. There are currently 10 action figures on the shelf.\n\nTo find out how many action figures Jerry initially had, we need to consider the changes made to the initial number:\n\n4. Let \\( x \\) be the initial number of action figures on the shelf.\n5. After adding 2 action figures, the number becomes \\( x + 2 \\).\n6. Then, Jerry removed 7 action figures, so the number becomes \\( x + 2 - 7 \\).\n7. We know that after these changes, there are 10 action figures on the shelf.\n\nTherefore, we can set up the equation:\n\n\\[ x + 2 - 7 = 10 \\]\n\n8. Simplify the equation:\n\n\\[ x - 5 = 10 \\]\n\n9. Solve for \\( x \\) by adding 5 to both sides:\n\n\\[ x = 10 + 5 \\]\n\n10. Therefore, \\( x = 15 \\).\n\nThe answer is that Jerry initially had 15 action figures on the shelf."

He has 15 books now.\n5. To find out how many books he sold, we subtract the number of books he currently has from the total number of books he should have had.\n6. Therefore, the number of books he sold is 63 - 15 = 48 books.\n7. He bought 42 new books.\n8. To find out how many more books he sold than he bought, we subtract the number of books he bought from the number of books he sold.\n9. Therefore, the number of more books he sold than he bought is 48 - 42 = 6.\n\nThe answer is 6."

To find out how many roses are left in the garden, we subtract the number of roses Jessica cut from the total number of roses originally in the garden.\n9. Therefore, the number of roses left in the garden is 12 - 8.\n10. Performing the subtraction, we get 12 - 8 = 4.\n\nThe answer is that Jessica cut 8 roses from her garden, and there are 4 roses left in the garden."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Jerry added 2 more action figures to the shelf.\n2. Jerry removed 7 of the old action figures from the shelf.\n3. There are currently 10 action figures on the shelf.\n\nTo find out how many action figures Jerry initially had, we need to consider the changes made to the initial number:\n\n4. Let \\( x \\) be the initial number of action figures on the shelf.\n5. After adding 2 action figures, the number becomes \\( x + 2 \\).\n6. Then, Jerry removed 7 action figures, so the number becomes \\( x + 2 - 7 \\).\n7. We know that after these changes, there are 10 action figures on the shelf.\n\nTherefore, we can set up the equation:\n\n\\[ x + 2 - 7 = 10 \\]\n\n8. Simplify the equation:\n\n\\[ x - 5 = 10 \\]\n\n9. Solve for \\( x \\) by adding 5 to both sides:\n\n\\[ x = 10 + 5 \\]\n\n10. Therefore, \\( x = 15 \\).\n\nThe answer is that Jerry initially had 15 action figures on the shelf."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. The book has a total of 23 pages.\n2. The first chapter is 10 pages long.\n\nGiven this information, we can directly determine the number of pages in the first chapter:\n\n3. The first chapter has 10 pages.\n\nThe answer is 10."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. The first chapter is 53 pages long.\n2. The third chapter is 21 pages long.\n3. To find out how many more pages the first chapter has than the third chapter, we subtract the number of pages in the third chapter from the number of pages in the first chapter.\n4. Therefore, the difference in pages is 53 - 21.\n5. Performing the subtraction, we get 53 - 21 = 32.\n\nThe answer is 32."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Dave initially had 21 apps on his phone.\n2. He added 89 new apps.\n3. Therefore, the total number of apps after adding is 21 + 89 = 110 apps.\n4. After deleting some apps, he had 24 apps left.\n5. To find out how many apps he deleted, we subtract the number of apps left from the total number of apps after adding.\n6. Therefore, the number of apps deleted is 110 - 24 = 86 apps.\n7. Dave added 89 apps and deleted 86 apps.\n8. To find out how many more apps he added than he deleted, we subtract the number of apps deleted from the number of apps added.\n9. Therefore, the number of more apps added than deleted is 89 - 86 = 3.\n\nThe answer is 3."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. Bobby initially had 36 pieces of candy.\n2. He ate 17 pieces of candy.\n3. After eating 17 pieces, the number of pieces left is 36 - 17.\n4. Performing the subtraction, we get 36 - 17 = 19 pieces left.\n5. Then, Bobby ate 15 more pieces of candy.\n6. To find out how many pieces he has left now, we subtract the 15 pieces he ate from the remaining 19 pieces.\n7. Therefore, the number of pieces of candy Bobby has left is 19 - 15.\n8. Performing the subtraction, we get 19 - 15 = 4.\n\nThe answer is 4 pieces of candy left."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. 20 bird families flew away for winter.\n2. 14 bird families stayed behind.\n3. To find the total number of bird families living near the mountain at the start, we need to add the number of families that flew away to the number of families that stayed behind.\n4. Therefore, the total number of bird families is 20 + 14.\n5. Performing the addition, we get 20 + 14 = 34.\n\nThe answer is 34 bird families were living near the mountain at the start."
"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. It took Frank 12 days to finish each book.\n2. Frank took a total of 492 days to finish all the books.\n3. To find out how many books Frank read, we need to divide the total number of days by the number of days it took to finish each book.\n4. Therefore, the number of books Frank read is 492 divided by 12.\n5. Performing the division, we get 492 / 12 = 41.\n\nThe answer is 41 books."

"Let's think step by step:\n\n1. The baker initially made 81 cakes.\n2. He then made an additional 92 cakes.\n3. To find the total number of cakes he made, we add the initial number of cakes to the additional cakes.\n4. Therefore, the total number of cakes made is 81 + 92.\n5. Performing the addition, we get 81 + 92 = 173 cakes.\n6. The baker sold 46 cakes.\n7. To find out how many more cakes the baker made than he sold, we subtract the number of cakes sold from the total number of cakes made.\n8. Therefore, the number of more cakes made than sold is 173 - 46.\n9. Performing the subtraction, we get 173 - 46 = 127.\n\nThe answer is 127."

Number of teachers in the school: 772\n\nTo find the total number of people in the school, we need to add the number of girls, boys, and teachers together.\n\n4. Total number of students (girls + boys) = 315 + 309\n5. Performing the addition, we get 315 + 309 = 624 students.\n\n6. Total number of people in the school (students + teachers) = 624 + 772\n7. Performing the addition, we get 624 + 772 = 1396 people.\n\nThe answer is 1396 people."

To find out how many boys she gave marbles to, we need to divide the total number of marbles by the number of marbles given to each boy.\n4. Therefore, the number of boys is 10 divided by 5.\n5. Performing the division, we get 10 / 5 = 2.\n\nThe answer is 2. Haley gave marbles to 2 boys."
